  /** Converts a <button> to look like an <a> tag. */
  .linkify {
    display: inline;
    padding: 0;
    margin: 0;
    border: 0;
    background: 0;
    cursor: pointer;
  }
  h1, h2, h3, h4 {
    background: none;

  a, chops-button, a.button, .button, .linkify {
    color: var(--chops-link-color);
    text-decoration: none;
    font-weight: var(--chops-link-font-weight);
    font-family: var(--chops-font-family);
  }
  a:hover, .linkify:hover {
    text-decoration: underline;
  }
  a.button, .button {
    /* Links that look like buttons. */
    display: inline-flex;
    align-items: center;
    justify-content: center;
    text-decoration: none;
    transition: filter 0.3s ease-in-out, box-shadow 0.3s ease-in-out;
  }
  a.button:hover, .button:hover {
    filter: brightness(95%);

  }

    display: block;

  textarea, select, input {
    box-sizing: border-box;
    font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
  }
  /* Note: decoupling heading levels from styles is useful for
  * accessibility because styles will not always line up with semantically
  * appropriate heading levels.

          --monorail-metadata-toggled-bg: var(--monorail-metadata-closed-bg);
        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;
        }
        .container-issue-content {
          padding: 0;
          flex-grow: 1;
          display: flex;
          align-items: stretch;

          box-sizing: border-box;
          padding-top: 0.5em;
        }

          box-sizing: border-box;
          width: 100%;
          max-width: 100%;
          margin: auto;
          padding: 0;
          display: flex;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: space-between;
          flex-direction: row;
          flex-wrap: no-wrap;
        }
        .container-no-issue {
          padding: 0.5em 16px;
          font-size: var(--chops-large-font-size);
        }
        .metadata-container {
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);

          border-right: var(--chops-normal-border);

          width: 24em;
          min-width: 256px;
          flex-grow: 0;
          flex-shrink: 0;
          box-sizing: border-box;
          z-index: 100;
        }
        .issue-header-container {
          z-index: 10;
          position: sticky;
          top: var(--monorail-header-height);
          margin-bottom: 0.25em;
          width: 100%;
        }

          min-width: 50%;
          max-width: 1000px;
          flex-grow: 1;
          box-sizing: border-box;
          min-height: 100%;

          padding-right: var(--mr-issue-page-horizontal-padding);
        }
        mr-issue-metadata {
          position: sticky;
          overflow-y: auto;
          top: var(--monorail-header-height);
          height: calc(100vh - var(--monorail-header-height));
        }
        mr-launch-overview {
          border-left: var(--chops-normal-border);

          }
          mr-issue-details, mr-launch-overview {
            width: 100%;

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>

        <p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





----------------------



<span class="line"><!---->----------------------<!----></span>



<br>





The PWA dialog has the "install" button focused by default. This presents an issue as this makes the dialog key-jackable,Bypassing Google Security measures in Chrome UI sensitive area `installing PWA` which lead to (user information disclosure without being aware) and 



<span class="line"><!---->The PWA dialog has the "install" button focused by default. This presents an issue as this makes the dialog key-jackable,Bypassing Google Security measures in Chrome UI sensitive area `installing PWA` which lead to (user information disclosure without being aware) and <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In a regular keyjacking attack (also works in this case), the Enter key would have to be pressed twice.



<span class="line"><!---->In a regular keyjacking attack (also works in this case), the Enter key would have to be pressed twice.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





What is likely happening (if key events are propagated `keydown`:



<span class="line"><!---->What is likely happening (if key events are propagated `keydown`:<!----></span>



<br>





1. The page listens for the Enter `keydown` event.



<span class="line"><!---->1. The page listens for the Enter `keydown` event.<!----></span>



<br>





2. The page opens a PWA dialog, with the 1st keyevent,and 2nd keypress accepts the install because it is default to install not cancel.



<span class="line"><!---->2. The page opens a PWA dialog, with the 1st keyevent,and 2nd keypress accepts the install because it is default to install not cancel.<!----></span>



<br>





3. The PWA dialog receives an Enter `keypress`, and the default confirm button is pressed.



<span class="line"><!---->3. The PWA dialog receives an Enter `keypress`, and the default confirm button is pressed.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





Impact:



<span class="line"><!---->Impact:<!----></span>



<br>





--------



<span class="line"><!---->--------<!----></span>



<br>





User Can be Tricked to press Enter key twice in game and Unknowingly install PWA Apps that could be Like legit Ones and user can provide passwords and sensitive data in , and send his data to Attacker C&C server without suspect as he didn't see accept/install button,nobody will send critical information to unknown sites. but this can be done here, in this case nobody are able to notice that they are sending their data to unknown attackers or non legit apps (user information disclosure without being aware) and ( Bypassing Google Security measures in Chrome UI sensitive area `installing PWA`).



<span class="line"><!---->User Can be Tricked to press Enter key twice in game and Unknowingly install PWA Apps that could be Like legit Ones and user can provide passwords and sensitive data in , and send his data to Attacker C&amp;C server without suspect as he didn't see accept/install button,nobody will send critical information to unknown sites. but this can be done here, in this case nobody are able to notice that they are sending their data to unknown attackers or non legit apps (user information disclosure without being aware) and ( Bypassing Google Security measures in Chrome UI sensitive area `installing PWA`).<!----></span>



<br>





 



<span class="line"><!----> <!----></span>



<br>

REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>





1. Host the attached files of simple PWA App on your Server and test , or simply Use Online Poc



<span class="line"><!---->1. Host the attached files of simple PWA App on your Server and test , or simply Use Online Poc<!----></span>



<br>





2. Navigate 



<span class="line"><!---->2. Navigate <!----></span>





https://vrphunt.com/chrome/spooforigin/a2hs-poc.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://vrphunt.com/chrome/spooforigin/a2hs-poc.html"><!---->https://vrphunt.com/chrome/spooforigin/a2hs-poc.html<!----></a>



<br>





3. Press `Enter twice immediately` , you will see PWA app installed and a new simple page Requesting Username and password.



<span class="line"><!---->3. Press `Enter twice immediately` , you will see PWA app installed and a new simple page Requesting Username and password.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Observed:



<span class="line"><!---->Observed:<!----></span>



<br>

<span class="line"><!---->---------<!----></span>



<br>





PWA dialog selects an install button by default Bypassing Google Security Measures in Chrome



<span class="line"><!---->PWA dialog selects an install button by default Bypassing Google Security Measures in Chrome<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Expected:



<span class="line"><!---->Expected:<!----></span>



<br>





---------



<span class="line"><!---->---------<!----></span>



<br>





According to References Below



<span class="line"><!---->According to References Below<!----></span>



<br>





# Don't have a default-selected accept button



<span class="line"><!----># Don't have a default-selected accept button<!----></span>



<br>





-PWA dialog should selects cancel button by default instead of install button.



<span class="line"><!---->-PWA dialog should selects cancel button by default instead of install button.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





References:



<span class="line"><!---->References:<!----></span>



<br>





============



<span class="line"><!---->============<!----></span>



<br>





Docs (docs/security/security-considerations-for-browser-ui.md):



<span class="line"><!---->Docs (docs/security/security-considerations-for-browser-ui.md):<!----></span>



<br>





> # Don't have a default-selected accept button



<span class="line"><!---->&gt; # Don't have a default-selected accept button<!----></span>



<br>





> If your dialog or UI has a call-to-action triggered by a button that is default-selected, the dialog is subject to keyjacking. An evil webpage can trick a user into mashing or repeatedly hitting the Enter key especially in games, and then trigger your dialog to show, causing the user to unknowingly accept and install the PWA. 



<span class="line"><!---->&gt; If your dialog or UI has a call-to-action triggered by a button that is default-selected, the dialog is subject to keyjacking. An evil webpage can trick a user into mashing or repeatedly hitting the Enter key especially in games, and then trigger your dialog to show, causing the user to unknowingly accept and install the PWA. <!----></span>



<br>



<br>

[dPWA] Make Cancel button default on PWA install dialogs.



<span class="line"><!---->[dPWA] Make Cancel button default on PWA install dialogs.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





To prevent keyjacking schemes, ensure that the Cancel button is set as



<span class="line"><!---->To prevent keyjacking schemes, ensure that the Cancel button is set as<!----></span>



<br>





the default button instead of the Accept one so that users spoofed



<span class="line"><!---->the default button instead of the Accept one so that users spoofed<!----></span>



<br>





with multiple Enter keys do not install a spoofed app by mistake.



<span class="line"><!---->with multiple Enter keys do not install a spoofed app by mistake.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The fix cannot be applied to the NONE button on the new detailed



<span class="line"><!---->The fix cannot be applied to the NONE button on the new detailed<!----></span>



<br>





installed dialog because the DialogBuilder does not allow making



<span class="line"><!---->installed dialog because the DialogBuilder does not allow making<!----></span>



<br>





buttons that are not implemented default.



<span class="line"><!---->buttons that are not implemented default.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

For M114 release:



<span class="line"><!---->For M114 release:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





1. This fixes a keyjacking medium security issue on the PWA installation dialog, and requires merging to stable channels after M112.



<span class="line"><!---->1. This fixes a keyjacking medium security issue on the PWA installation dialog, and requires merging to stable channels after M112.<!----></span>



<br>





2. This is the fix that will be merged: 



<span class="line"><!---->2. This is the fix that will be merged: <!----></span>





https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/4505003



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/4505003"><!---->https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/4505003<!----></a>



<br>





3. Yes, the changes have been released and tested on canary.



<span class="line"><!---->3. Yes, the changes have been released and tested on canary.<!----></span>



<br>





4. No, this is not behind a Finch Flag.



<span class="line"><!---->4. No, this is not behind a Finch Flag.<!----></span>



<br>





5. +jinrongwu@ fyi



<span class="line"><!---->5. +jinrongwu@ fyi<!----></span>



<br>





6. This requires a fix to Stable, so manual testing steps:



<span class="line"><!---->6. This requires a fix to Stable, so manual testing steps:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





For the normal installation bubble:



<span class="line"><!---->For the normal installation bubble:<!----></span>



<br>





1. Navigate to 



<span class="line"><!---->1. Navigate to <!----></span>





https://vrphunt.com/chrome/spooforigin/a2hs-poc.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://vrphunt.com/chrome/spooforigin/a2hs-poc.html"><!---->https://vrphunt.com/chrome/spooforigin/a2hs-poc.html<!----></a>



<br>





2. Wait for app to finish loading, press enter twice.



<span class="line"><!---->2. Wait for app to finish loading, press enter twice.<!----></span>



<br>





3. Verify app is not installed on chrome://apps (the first enter focuses on the omnibox icon and clicks on it, the 2nd enter opens the installation dialog and closes it).



<span class="line"><!---->3. Verify app is not installed on chrome://apps (the first enter focuses on the omnibox icon and clicks on it, the 2nd enter opens the installation dialog and closes it).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





For the detailed PWA installation bubble:



<span class="line"><!---->For the detailed PWA installation bubble:<!----></span>



<br>





1. Navigate to 



<span class="line"><!---->1. Navigate to <!----></span>





https://squoosh.app/



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://squoosh.app/"><!---->https://squoosh.app/<!----></a>



<br>





2. Wait for app to finish loading, and press tab to navigate to the omnibox install icon.



<span class="line"><!---->2. Wait for app to finish loading, and press tab to navigate to the omnibox install icon.<!----></span>



<br>





3. Once the icon is highlighted, press enter twice.



<span class="line"><!---->3. Once the icon is highlighted, press enter twice.<!----></span>



<br>





4. Verify app is not installed on chrome://apps.



<span class="line"><!---->4. Verify app is not installed on chrome://apps.<!----></span>

For the normal installation bubble:



<span class="line"><!---->For the normal installation bubble:<!----></span>



<br>





1. Navigate to 



<span class="line"><!---->1. Navigate to <!----></span>





https://vrphunt.com/chrome/spooforigin/a2hs-poc.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://vrphunt.com/chrome/spooforigin/a2hs-poc.html"><!---->https://vrphunt.com/chrome/spooforigin/a2hs-poc.html<!----></a>



<br>





2. Wait for app to finish loading, press enter twice.



<span class="line"><!---->2. Wait for app to finish loading, press enter twice.<!----></span>



<br>





3. Verify app is not installed on chrome://apps (the first enter focuses on the omnibox icon and clicks on it, the 2nd enter opens the installation dialog and closes it).



<span class="line"><!---->3. Verify app is not installed on chrome://apps (the first enter focuses on the omnibox icon and clicks on it, the 2nd enter opens the installation dialog and closes it).<!----></span>

https://squoosh.app/

<br>

<span class="line"><!---->2. Wait for app to finish loading, and press tab to navigate to the omnibox install icon.<!----></span>



<br>





3. Once the icon is highlighted, press enter twice.



<span class="line"><!---->3. Once the icon is highlighted, press enter twice.<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->4. Verify app is not installed on chrome://apps.<!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.

        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */

          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;

          position: absolute;

          width: 1px;
